-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
for i,Prt in pairs(game:GetDescendants()) do
pcall(function()
if string.match(Prt.Name,"Admin") or string.match(Prt.Name,"Essentials") then
PrtBig Grinestroy()
end
end)
end

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
